### Round 1 | planner | planner_initial

- diagnosis: The task is to assess the likely AIE mechanism from the provided molecule. From SMILES-only evidence, the current top1 working hypothesis is ICT and the current top2 runner-up is TICT. ESIPT remains an additional credible portfolio member because the molecule contains a phenolic OH together with nearby nitrogen-containing acceptor functionality, so the case cannot yet be collapsed to a pure ICT-versus-TICT framing. ICT is only a working hypothesis because donor-acceptor segmentation is visible at the motif level, but the actual excited-state pathway could still depend on twisting or proton-transfer preorganization that SMILES alone cannot resolve. The main visible uncertainty is that the same heteroatom-rich conjugated scaffold that supports ICT also contains several rotatable connections supporting TICT plausibility, while the OH/N motif leaves ESIPT chemically plausible until screened. Shared prepared structure context is available and ready for downstream execution, but per the initial-stage rule it is not used here as first-layer mechanism evidence. Macro can provide bounded structural screening from one deterministic registry-backed capability, but it cannot make a global mechanism judgment. Microscopic can perform one low-cost baseline S0/S1 action on the shared prepared structure, which can supply indirect electronic-state evidence, but it cannot in round 1 run conformer sensitivity, torsion scans, or a multi-step ESIPT workflow. Both macro and microscopic evidence should be gathered in the first round because structural topology and baseline S0/S1 observables address different uncertainty sources. The case therefore remains in portfolio screening rather than pairwise contraction.

- action: macro_and_microscopic

- confidence: 0.38

- task_instruction: Run one deterministic macro screen focused on donor-acceptor layout, and one bounded microscopic baseline S0/S1 action on the shared prepared structure, with both reports framed as evidence to screen ICT, TICT, and ESIPT portfolio uncertainty rather than to finalize mechanism.

### Round 1 | macro | run_macro

- agent_name: macro

- status: success

- task_received: Current reasoning phase: portfolio_screening. Agent framing mode: portfolio_neutral. The current_hypothesis 'ICT' is only a provisional top1 for bookkeeping in this stage. First-round macro and microscopic tasks will provide only indirect evidence but can reduce coverage debt efficiently. Task: Assess macro-level structural evidence relevant to the current working hypothesis 'ICT'. Reuse the shared prepared structure context when available, summarize low-cost structural indicators only, and stay within current macro capability. Hypothesis uncertainty to keep in mind: ICT leads because of clear donor-acceptor motif evidence in the SMILES, but that same scaffold leaves unresolved whether excited-state twisting is central and whether the OH/N arrangement is sufficiently preorganized for ESIPT; direct screening of those alternatives has not yet occurred.

- task_completion_status: completed

- task_completion: Task completed successfully within current macro capability.

- task_understanding: The task is to assess macro-level structural evidence relevant to the current working hypothesis 'ICT' by summarizing low-cost structural indicators from the shared prepared structure context. The goal is to provide indirect evidence that can help screen the ICT hypothesis against alternatives like TICT and ESIPT without anchoring the analysis solely on ICT.

- reasoning_summary: Given the current hypothesis ICT is provisional and the screening focus includes TICT and ESIPT, the macro structural evidence should focus on donor-acceptor layout, rotor and torsion topology, planarity and compactness, and intramolecular hydrogen bond preorganization. - task_completion_status: completed

- task_understanding: The task is to execute the registry-backed macro capability 'screen_intramolecular_hbond_preorganization' to inspect the shared prepared molecular geometry for evidence of intramolecular hydrogen bond preorganization, specifically phenolic OH-to-imine or related donor/acceptor contacts. This aims to directly address the remaining coverage debt for the ESIPT hypothesis by determining if there is concrete intramolecular H-bond candidate and local transfer-compatible geometry present or absent.

- reasoning_summary: The current portfolio screening phase has cleared the TICT hypothesis at the structural level via rotor/torsion topology screening, but ESIPT remains unresolved due to lack of direct evidence for intramolecular H-bond preorganization. Prior macro screening indirectly weakened ESIPT by absence of explicit H-bond cues, but a single conformer does not fully exclude alternative arrangements. Therefore, a focused deterministic macro capability using the shared prepared geometry is needed to provide bounded direct evidence for or against ESIPT's intramolecular H-bond preorganization.
Capability limit note: This macro capability relies on the availability of the shared prepared geometry context. Without it, only motif-level fallback screening would be possible, which is not requested here. The capability is deterministic and bounded to single-molecule structural evidence and cannot adjudicate excited-state dynamics or aggregation effects.

### Round 5 | macro | run_macro

- agent_name: macro

- status: success

- task_received: Current reasoning phase: portfolio_screening. Agent framing mode: portfolio_neutral. Do not treat TICT as settled. Execute exactly one registry-backed macro capability: `screen_donor_acceptor_layout`. The purpose is to directly screen the remaining coverage-debt hypothesis ICT on its own terms. Use the available structural context to summarize donor-acceptor segmentation, conjugation-level layout, and donor-acceptor partition proxy. Report only bounded structural evidence relevant to whether ICT has direct support or is further weakened relative to TICT; do not make the global mechanism decision.

- task_completion_status: completed

- task_completion: Task completed successfully within current macro capability.

- task_understanding: The task is to perform a deterministic macro-level structural screening focused on the ICT hypothesis by executing the registry-backed macro capability 'screen_donor_acceptor_layout'. This involves analyzing the available shared prepared molecular structure to summarize donor-acceptor segmentation, conjugation-level layout, and donor-acceptor partition proxy. The goal is to collect bounded structural evidence that directly supports or weakens the ICT hypothesis relative to TICT, without making any global mechanism adjudication or final decision.

- reasoning_summary: Previous rounds have directly screened TICT and weakened ESIPT, leaving ICT as the main unresolved credible alternative without direct positive evidence. The shared prepared structure context is available and suitable for deterministic macro analysis. By screening donor-acceptor layout, we can obtain direct structural evidence relevant to ICT's plausibility, helping to reduce portfolio coverage debt. This approach is consistent with the portfolio_neutral framing and portfolio_screening phase, focusing on bounded structural evidence without global adjudication.
Capability limit note: The macro capability is limited to deterministic, low-cost single-molecule structural analysis using the shared prepared structure context. It cannot resolve excited-state dynamics, aggregation effects, or global mechanism adjudication. If the shared prepared structure is unavailable, a SMILES-only fallback would be used, but here the shared structure is available.

- execution_plan: Use deterministic_macro_structure_scan to execute the bounded registry-backed macro capability `screen_donor_acceptor_layout` with focus areas: donor-acceptor segmentation, conjugation-level layout, donor-acceptor partition proxy. Planned local steps: [shared_context_load] Load the shared prepared structure context and reuse its descriptors. [focus_selection] Translate the Planner instruction into one bounded registry-backed macro capability. [topology_analysis] Collect deterministic structural evidence for `screen_donor_acceptor_layout` from the available structure source. [geometry_proxy_analysis] Summarize only bounded local structural or geometry-proxy outputs and record any missing deliverables.

- result_summary: Bounded donor-acceptor layout screening summarized donor/acceptor partition, hetero-atom burden, and conjugation-level layout from the available structural context.
